elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<p>Make crust:<br> 1. Grease a 6cm-deep, 20cm-round (base) springform pan.<br> 2. Process biscuits until mixture resembles fine breadcrumbs.<br> 3. Add butter. Process until just combined.<br> 4. Press mixture over base and side of prepared pan.<br> <br> Make topping:<br> 1. Stir blueberry spread in low heat until melted.<br> <br> Make filling:<br> 1. Using electric mixer, beat cream cheese and sugar in large bowl until until smooth.<br> 2. Add sour cream.<br> 3. Add eggs 1 at a time.<br> 4. Sift the flour.<br> 5. Pour the filling on top of the base<br> 6. Bake cheesecake in 170C for 1 hours, the cake is slightly puffed and golden brown.<br> 7. Refrigerate until cold.<br> 8. Smooth top with the topping over the cheesecake.</p>
elements.author.elementType=text
elements.author.value=Linda Hou
elements.link.elementType=link
elements.description.elementType=formattedtext
elements.description.value=<p>Delicious easy to make blueberry cheesecake for all occasions.</p>
elements.ingredients.elementType=formattedtext
elements.ingredients.value=<p>For crust:<br> 80g digestive biscuits<br> 40g butter, melted</p> 
<p>For topping:<br> 1/3 blueberry spread<br> <br> For filling:<br> 250g Philadelphia cheese block, softened<br> 2 large eggs<br> 40g sugar<br> 15g all purpose flour<br> 100g sour cream<br> &nbsp;</p>

elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>Heat butter over medium heat in a large saucepan.</li>
 <li>Add onion and garlic and saute for 3-4 minutes until tender.</li>
 <li>Add the peas and saute a minute more.</li>
 <li>Pour in the stock and simmer for 3-4 minutes until the peas are just tender.</li>
 <li>Blend the mixture until smooth. Add a litte more water if you prefer a thinner soup.</li>
 <li>Serve with bay leaf and a swirl of creme fraiche.</li>
</ol>

elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>Combine all the ingredients, except the chicken, in a bowl and mix together.</li>
 <li>Set aside 1/3 of the marinade to be used later.</li>
 <li>Place chicken breasts in the marinade and marinate from 4 hours to overnight.</li>
 <li>Preheat the grill to medium heat and oil it.</li>
 <li>Grill chicken until it is cooked through, about 5 minutes on each side.</li>
 <li>Brush chicken with the reserved marinade mix occasionally.</li>
 <li>Remove chicken from the grill, and wrap with foil. Allow to cool for 5 minutes before serving.</li>
</ol>

elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>Peel and chop the medium mango. Use a blender to puree the mango pieces until smooth.</li>
 <li>Beat the cream cheese in a bowl until smooth with an electric mixer on low speed.</li>
 <li>Add in the heavy cream, powdered sugar and gelatin. Beat the mixture on medium speed until it thickens.</li>
 <li>Fold in the mango puree and refrigerate for at least two hours.</li>
 <li>To serve, assemble in small cups with layers of shortbread cookies and mango cream mixture. Then top with chocolate flakes.</li>
</ol>

elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>Fry the sliced beef in a wok for three minutes and set aside on a plate when done.</li>
 <li>Heat the wok over high heat.</li>
 <li>Pour beaten egg into wok, stirring constantly. Cook for 2 minutes until eggs are a little scrambled.</li>
 <li>Add sliced beef and stir for 1 minute.</li>
 <li>Next add the leftover rice and stir fry for another 3 minutes.</li>
 <li>Add soy sauce and sesame oil and stir fry for another 3 minutes.</li>
 <li>Sprinkle with chopped spring onions and serve.</li>
</ol>

elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>Preheat oven to 375°F (190°C).</li>
 <li>Cut bread diagonally into thick slices.</li>
 <li>Brush each slice with a thin layer of olive oil on both sides and place on baking sheet.</li>
 <li>Bake the slices of bread 5-7 minutes on each side until golden brown.</li>
 <li>Remove from oven and sprinkle with pepper jack cheese. Serve warm.</li>
</ol>

elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>Chop chocolate into small pieces and combine it with the cream in a bowl.</li>
 <li>Heat the chocolate and cream in a microwave for 2 to 3 minutes on 50% power, stirring every minute.</li>
 <li>When the mixture is melted and smooth, stir in coffee powder.</li>
 <li>Cover the bowl with plastic wrap and refrigerate for 3 hours until firm.</li>
 <li>Roll the chocolate mixture into balls, using 2 teaspoons at a time.</li>
 <li>Coat the truffles in chocolate sprinkles and serve, or refrigerate for later.</li>
</ol>

elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>Preheat oven to 200°C.</li>
 <li>Line a 12 hole muffin tray with muffin cases.</li>
 <li>Sift the self raising flour into a large bowl. Add sugar and stir together to form a dry mixture.</li>
 <li>In a separate bowl, whisk egg, milk and vegetable oil together to form a liquid mixture.</li>
 <li>Gently pour the liquid mixture into the bowl of dry mixture. Stir with a spoon until slightly lumpy, without over-mixing.</li>
 <li>Evenly fold in blueberries.</li>
 <li>Divide mixture evenly into the muffin cases and sprinkle sugar on top.</li>
 <li>Bake for 25 minutes until lightly golden.</li>
 <li>Allow to cool for 5 minutes in muffin tray, before transferring to wire rack.</li>
</ol>

elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>Take the steak from the packet and dry it out with paper towel.</li>
 <li>Cover the steak liberally with salt and pepper.</li>
 <li>Put the steak in the fridge on a rack for 6 hours to encourage it to dry out. This will enhance the flavour, and the salt will be pulled into the steak.</li>
 <li>Heat the flatplate part of your bbq and put the steak on the opposite side, and then close the bbq lid.</li>
 <li>Put the ghee in a bowl and leave it in the unheated side of the bbq to melt.</li>
 <li>Check the steak every 5 minutes with an instant read thermometer. When it reaches 45 degrees celsius, dump it in the ghee.</li>
 <li>Brown the steak up on the flatplate, turning every 10 seconds, and liberally dunking it in the melted ghee.</li>
 <li>When it is suitably browned, take the steak off the grill, place on a warmed plate and cover tightly with aluminium foil.</li>
 <li>After 10 minutes, it is ready. Serve with roast potatoes, steamed green beans and dijon mustard.</li>
</ol>

elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>Cook the spaghetti in a large pot of boiling salted water, according to package instructions. While it is simmering, make the shrimp and sauce.</li>
 <li>Season shrimp with salt and pepper.</li>
 <li>Add olive oil and 1 tablespoon of butter in a frying pan over medium high heat. Add minced garlic and cook for about 2 minutes, and then add parsley.</li>
 <li>Add shrimp and cook for about 2 to 3 minutes until evenly cooked and pink on each side.</li>
 <li>Melt remaining 2 tablespoons of butter and stir a little of the water from pasta that is cooking. Keep warm until spaghetti is ready.</li>
 <li>Drain the spaghetti and serve in bowls with shrimp and sauce on top. Enjoy!</li>
</ol>

elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>Heat butter over medium heat in a large saucepan.</li>
 <li>Add onion and garlic and saute for 3-4 minutes until tender.</li>
 <li>Add pumpkin and potatoes and saute for 5 more minutes.</li>
 <li>Pour in the stock and simmer for 15-20 minutes until the potatoes are just tender.</li>
 <li>Blend the mixture until smooth. Add a little more water if you prefer a thinner soup.</li>
 <li>Serve with chopped chives.</li>
</ol>

elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>In a jug, whisk eggs and milk.</li>
 <li>In a bowl, sift flour and add in sugar.</li>
 <li>Add milk mixture into the bowl and whisk until smooth and lump free.</li>
 <li>Heat a large frying pan over medium heat and brush with butter over cooking surface.</li>
 <li>Pour 1/4 cup of mixture for each pancake and cook for 2 minutes or when bubbles form on the surface. Flip the pancake over and cook for another 2 minutes or when lightly golden.</li>
 <li>Serve with maple syrup.</li>
</ol>

elements.ingredients.value=<p>2 eggs<br> 1 3/4 cup milk<br> 2 cups self-raising flour<br> 1/3 cup sugar<br> 50g butter<br> Maple syrup</p>

elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>Wash and hull the raspberries.</li>
 <li>Spoon one layer of granola at the bottom of a cup.</li>
 <li>Add a layer of Greek yogurt and raspberries.</li>
 <li>Repeat the layering until cup is full.</li>
 <li>Store in refrigerator until ready to serve.</li>
</ol>

elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>Pour the 6 cups of water in a large saucepan, add salt and boil over medium high heat.</li>
 <li>Add squid and cook for 3 minutes until tender. Remove squid with a slotted spoon and drain in ice water. Cut squid into small pieces and place in a large bowl.</li>
 <li>Add shrimp to boiling water and cook for 3 minutes until tender. Remove squid with a slotted spoon and drain in ice water. Place squid in the large bowl with squid.</li>
 <li>Add octopus to simmering water and simmer for 2 hours until tender. Remove octopus with a slotted spoon and drain in ice water. Cut octopus into small pieces and place in the large bowl.</li>
 <li>Add crab stick meat to the bowl of seafood mixture.</li>
 <li>Finely chop the fresh herbs.</li>
 <li>Add the herbs, olive oil, lemon juice and minced garlic into the seafood bowl. Toss to combine.</li>
 <li>Transfer to a plate and serve with lemon wedges as garnish.</li>
</ol>
elements.author.elementType=text
elements.author.value=Linda Hou
elements.link.elementType=link
elements.description.elementType=formattedtext
elements.description.value=<p>A very quick and versatile pasta-free seafood salad. This is a basic recipe - feel free to add your own spin (grated carrots, diced green or red capsicums, red cabbage, seasonings).</p>
elements.ingredients.elementType=formattedtext
elements.ingredients.value=<p>6 cups water<br> 1 tsp salt<br> 300g squid, cleaned<br> 300g shrimp, peeled and deveined<br> 300g octopus, cleaned &nbsp;<br> 300g crab stick meat, chopped<br> 1/4 cup fresh lemon juice<br> &nbsp;3 cups mixed fresh herb leaves (mint, basil, parsley)<br> 2 tbsp extra virgin olive oil<br> 2 garlic cloves, minced<br> Lemon wedges</p>

elements.method.elementType=formattedtext
elements.method.value=<ol>
 <li>In a bowl, mix the pork, egg, flour, cabbage and scallions to make the filling mixture.</li>
 <li>Scoop 1tbsp of mixture into the middle of a dumpling sheet. Adjust the amount of filling depending on size of your sheets.</li>
 <li>Fold the sheet in half and press the edges together to seal the mixture inside. If you find that the edges don't stick easily, adding a small amount of water or egg yolk to the edge before pressing may help. Repeat until all of the mixture is used up.</li>
 <li>Place the dumplings inside a steamer pot and steam for 15 minutes or until the dumpling skin becomes soft and slightly translucent.</li>
 <li>To make the dipping sauce, mix the soy sauce, sugar and a few scallion pieces in a small dish. Ensure that the sugar has been completely disolved before serving.</li>
 <li>Enjoy!</li>
</ol>
elements.author.elementType=text
elements.author.value=Clarissa Wisan
